@# / /
man ngag rnam gsum gyi skor bzhugs so / /
@## / /
lcags ra ngag dbang 'phrin las dpal bzang gis mdzad zhi ba'i 'khor lo bsgrub tshul nyes tshogs rgud mun sel ba phan bde'i nyi ma gsar ba'i 'gor| bstan pa'i 'khor lo bdud sde'i gshed gnyid du /

! thar rtse nam mkha' dpal bzang gis mdzad pa'i sbyong rgyud dkyil chog gzhan phan rgya mtsho dang /
snga sprul 'jam dbyangs thub bstan nyi mas mdzad pa'i kun rig gi sgrub dkyil gung bsgrigs pa'i steng nas sbyong rgyud dkyil 'khor bcu gnyis kyi dbang mnos pa'i thod 'god par /
sta gon gcig 'thugs kyis byang chu kyi sems mtshon pa kun rig rtsa ba'i dkyil 'khor /
sdig pa 'joms byed gtsug dgu 'am shAkya thub pa sku'i dkyil 'khor /
'di spyi bka' rdor 'phreng na yod /
'chi ba bzlog byed phyag rdor 'chi bdag 'joms pa thugs kyi dkyil 'khor /
tshe yun ring bsring bar byed pa tshe dpag med gsung gi dkyil 'khor /
'phrin las rgya cher sgrub byed 'khor los bsgyur ba yon tan gyi dkyil 'khor /
ma rung ba tshar gcod byed me ltar 'bar ba 'phrin las kyi dkyil 'khor te 'jigs rten las 'das pa'i dkyil 'khor drug /
bar chad zhi byed gtso bo phyag na rdo rje la rgyal chen bzhis bskor ba'i dkyil 'khor /

tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtsho'i yig cha'i steng nas ras chung ba nas brgyud pa'i padma gar dbang gi rigs su gtogs pa'i rta mgrin dmar po dbyug pa can gyi rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni /

rje rgyal ba gnyis pa tsong kha pa chen po'i thugs bcud byang chub lam gyi rim pa chen mo'i tshig rkyang gi lung dang zhib bshad sbrags pa'i bshad lung rgyas pa thob pa'i brgyud pa gong ma lam rim gsol 'debs lam mchog sgo 'byed du gsal ba ltar la /

byang chu kyi sems la blo sbyong tshul gyi man ngag blo sbyong don bdun ma'i khrid rgyal sras thogs med dpal bzang gi khrid yig gi steng nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni /

mnga' ris glo bo rje btsun kun dga' grol mchog gis 'bad pa du mas btsal ba'i mdo sngags sna tshogs kyi khrid brgya rtsa brgyad phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa jo nang khrid brgya rtsar grags pa'i skor la /
nub pa rig 'dzin grags pa dang sa paN gyi yi ge las btus pa'i rje btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyis sa chen kun snying la gnang ba blo sbyon zhen pa bzhi bral gyi khrid /
rgyal sras thogs med kyi gsung las btus pa blo sbyong don bdun ma'i khrid /
mus chen rgyal mtshan dpal bzang gi khrid yig las btus pa'i rten 'brel snying po'i khrid /
rgyal sras chos rdzong ba'i gsung las bla ma red mda' pa'i @# / /
zin bris mdzad pa las btus pa'i skyid sdug lam 'khyer gyi khrid /
bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyi khrid yig las btus pa'i sum pa lo tsA pa'i blo sbyong gi khrid /

khro phu lo tsA pa'i yi ge las btus pa'i snying po don gsum gyi khrid /
yang rtse pa rin chen seng+ge'i khrid yig las btus pa'i sems nyid ngal bso'i khrid /
mchims nam mkha'i grags kyi khrid yig las btus pa'i skyes bu gsum gyi khrid /
mchims kyi yi ge las btus pa'i bstan rim gyi khrid /
mchims kyi yi ge las btus pa'i srid zhi'i mnyam nyid kyi khrid /
byang sems zla ba rgyal mtshan gyi khrid yig las btus pa'i dbu ma chen po'i khrid /
mchims kyi yig rnying las btus pa'i bka' gdams lkog khrid /
yig rnying las btus pa'i bka' gdams lha bzhi'i thub pa'i khrid /
mchims kyi khrid las btus pa'i spyan ras gzigs kyi khrid /
yig rnying las btus pa'i lha bzhi'i mi g.yo ba'i khrid /
mchims kyi khrid yig las btus pa'i lha bzhi'i sgrol ma'i khrid /
hor dka' bzhi pa'i khrid dpe las btus pa'i po to pa'i dpe chos kyi khrid /
glegs bam rang dang gnyug la paN chen gyi khrid yig las btus pa'i bka' gdams thig le bcu drug gi khrid /
rong ston shAkya rgyal mtshan gyi yi ge las btus pa'i sher phyin bka' babs drug gi khrid /
rong ston shes bya kun rig gi khrid yig las btus pa'i zhi byed lam lnga'i khrid /
rong ston gyi khrid yig las btus pa'i sgom rim thog mtha' bar gsum gyi khrid /
bcom ldan rigs pa'i ral gri'i khrid dpe las btus pa'i byams chos lnga'i khrid /
ba tshab lo tsA pa'i khrid yig las btus pa'i rang stong gi khrid /
btsan kha po che'i yig rnying las btus ba'i gzhan stong gi khrid /
kun dga' grol mchog rang gi rgyas 'grel las btus pa'i po dong phyogs rgyal ba'i de nyid 'dus pa'i snying po khol du phyung pa sbas don gyi khrid /
grol mchog rang gi khrid yig las btus pa'i grub rgyal tshe khrid /
gsung rgyun las byung ba'i jo bo lugs sgrol dkar gyi khrid /
chag lo'i khrid yig las btus pa'i tshe dpag med dkar po'i khrid /
chos rje sher 'bum pa'i khrid yig las btus pa'i tshem bu dmar khrid /
yol ston chos dbang gi yi ge rnying ba las btus pa'i dpal mo lugs kyi dmar khrid /
'dzim chen @# / /
dang rong ston gyi khrid dpe las btus pa'i dmar khrid zla rgyal lugs /
chos sku shAkya rin chen gyi khrid yig las btus pa'i dmar khrid sgyer sgrang lugs / /
gsung rgyun las bris pa'i bde mchog dmar khrid /
gsung rgyun ltar bris pa'i kyai rdor dmar khrid /
dmar gya'i yig rnying las btus pa'i phyag rdor 'khor chen bskyed rdzogs kyi khrid /

gces bsdus las btus pa'i ku ru ku l+le'i khrid /

mgos kyi stong thun shog dril @# / /

zhang lo'i @# / /

khyab bdag 'khor lo'i mgon po rje dge 'dun bstan 'dzin rgya mtsho dpal bzang po /
des bdag la'o / /
yang na /
thang sag pa dngos grub rgya ma mtsho yan sngar ltar la /
de nas zhogs don yod mkhas grub /
dpon slob ngag dbang byams pa /
yongs 'dzin ye shes rgyal mtshan /
shing bza' rin po che blo bzang dar rgyas rgya mtsho /
rje gser khang thams cad mkhyen pa /
bka' drin mtshungs med rje blo bzang lung rigs rgya mtsho dpal bzang po /
des bdag la'o / /
@# / /
yang na /
yongs 'dzin rin po che blo bzang tshul khrims byams pa rgya mtsho dpal bzang po'i zhal snga nas khrid yig dngos grub kun 'byung gi steng nas lan gcig thob /
! yang na /
shing bza' paN+Di ta blo bzang bstan pa'i dbang phyug tshul khrims phun tshogs kyi zhal snga nas kyang khrid lung bcas lan gcig thob pa'i brgyud pa ni snga ma dang 'dra /
! /
yang na /
dka' chen byang chub rin chen gyi zhal snga nas kyang skyabs 'gro tshad med bzhi dga' lha dang bcas kyi khrid kyang thob bo / /

dga' ldan lha brgya ma'i 'pho khrid dmigs brtse ma 'bum gyi bka' rgya can gyi khrid rgyun ni /

de nas khri bsod nams dbang rgyal /

des bdag la'o / /

paN chen blo bzang chos kyi rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i 'od dpag med la brten pa'i 'pho ba le tshan gnyis gung bsgrigs pa'i steng nas dpa' po g.yul 'jug ma'i 'pho khrid mnos pa'i brgyud pa ni /
rgyal ba rdo rje 'chang /
rje btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs /
dbu ma pa dpa' bo rdo rje /
chos kyi rgyal po tsong kha pa pa chen po /
mkhas grub dge legs dpal bzang /
ba so chos kyi rgyal mtshan /
grub chen chos kyi rdo rje /
rgyal ba blo bzang don grub /
mkhas grub sangs rgyas ye shes /

bka' drin mtshungs med rje btsun dge 'dun bstan 'dzin rgya mtsho dpal bzang po /
des bdag la'o / /
! yang na /

red 'da' pa dang /

()nya() par dmigs brtse ma'i las tshogs dngos grub char 'bebs rje 'jam dbyangs dga' ba'i blo gros kyis mdzad par grags pa la rje don grub rgyal mtshan gyis phra btab byas pa /

mtshan gyis mdzad pa bcas la shog /
()ta() par rje bla ma la brten pa'i ril sgrub bsam 'phel dbang gi rgyal po khri chen rgya nag pa blo bzang bstan pa'i nyi mas mdzad pa /

()da() par rje bla ma rigs gsum spyi sgrub la brten nas sa bcud gso ba'i lha klu'i bum pa gcig 'thus su sgrub pa'i bca' sgrig sgrub sbas kyi cho ga'i 'khrigs sdebs byin rlabs 'od stong 'dren pa'i ngo mtshar skya rengs gsar ba shar chen ngag dbang tshul khrims kyis mdzad pa la shog /

()pa() par dmigs brtse ma'i sgo nas bkru byabs bsrung ba bya tshul gdung sel bdud rtsi'i chu rgyun rje dkon mchog rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa la shog8 /
()pha() par srad brgyud lugs kyi dga' ldan 'pho khrid kyi brjed byang mi pham bla ma'i zhal lung rje shes rab rgya mtshos mdzad pa /

()ba() bar rje bla ma tsong kha pa chen po la stong mchod 'bul ba'i cho ga kun bzang 'khri shing che shos sprul sku ngag dbang bshad sgrub bstan pa'i nyi mas mdzad pa /

()tsha() par rje bdag nyid chen po sogs kyi sku brnyan 'ga' zhig gi lo rgyus cung zad brjod pa mnyan par bos pa'i gtam gyi phreng brje shes rab rgya mtshos mdzad pa la shog /
()dza() par lha gcig rdo rje 'chang ye shes don grub bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i spyod tshul gyi rnam bshad tshe 'di'i snang gnyid sangs byed yid bzhin nor bu rje 'jam dbyangs 'phrin las kyis mdzad pa la shog25 /
()wa() par lha mo 'od zer can ma'i sgrub thabs dang 'khor lo'i las tshogs thun mong ma yin pa rgya can skyid shod ngag dbang bstan 'dzin 'phrin las kyis mdzad pa la shog /
()zha() par dus gsum sangs rgyas thams cad kyi ngo bo rgyal ba blo bzang grags pa la gsol ba 'debs pa'i smon tshig bsam pa lhun gyis 'grub pa rgyal mkhan po grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa la shog4 /

(ja) yan lag bdun pa dge slong ma dpal mos mdzad pa /
(nya) slob dpon bsod nams rtse mos mdzad pa'i bkra shis /

mdzod kyi mtha' can /
'dar phyar ru pa rin chen dpal bzang gis brag dmar chos grwar mdzad pa'i bskang bar dmar khrag chang ma /

a mo g+has mdzad pa'i bskang ba dus gsum rgyal bam /

lcang spel ba seng+ge 'bum gyis mdzad pa'i bskang ba byang shar dbang ldan ma /

bu d+ha b+ha dras bstod pa'i gnod sbyin zangs kyi beg rtse ma /

gnod sbyin lcam dral gyi thugs dam bskang ba'i cho ga rgyas pa byang shar mya ngan ma (bde) shar mdo khams pa rdo rje bkra shis kyi ngor rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rjes mdzad pa /
des Atsar+ya nyi 'od grags pa dang nyan lo gong ma rnams kyi yi ge 'thor bu phyogs gcig tu bsdebs te mdzad pa'i (bde) gnod sbyin lcam dral gyi las byang 'phrin las lhun grub ma /
gtor mdos la brten nas srog bdag dmar po bshan pa sgrol byed bcos pa'i (bde shri) thabs phyogs phyogs ma gnyan lo ts+tsha bas mdzad pa srog bdag dmar po'i bskang mdos rdzogs so'i mtha' can /
gnod sbyin lcam dral 'khor bcas kyi phyi rten btsugs pa'i lag len gyi rim pa gnyag gi ban+de bi ja ya b+ha dras dpal gnyan lo'i gtsug lag khang du mdzad pa /

phur bar brten nas cho 'phrul rnams gtong ba /
'gor srog bdag bshan pa zhes yod pa'i dmod kha brgyad pa ithi'i mtha' can /
'gor srog bdag chen po'i dus la babs zhes yod pa'i (bde) bla 'gugs pho nya'i skabs gtso bo rnams kyi bskul byang bskul zhing rbad do rdzogs so'i mtha' can rnams drag po btsan gyi rgyal 'bud slob dpon chen po'i mnga' bdag la gdams pa spa gro skyor chung dang ru lag grums pa rkyang gnyis su rgod dang /
g.yung mar yul du sbas shing rgod gcig mchims phur sbas pa mdag bdag nyang gis spyan drangs pa bshan pa srog gcod dmar po'i srog mthu drag po btsan gyi rgyal 'bud bsnyen sgrub rbad bskul la ma ltos pa'i ngan sngags chig chod ma yid la yang dran du mi rung ngo'i mtha' can /
gsang bskul dur khrod chen po ma 'phrin las gong ma rnams las thos pa yi ge bkod pa'o'i mtha' can /
'di ma thob /
bshan pa srog gcod dmar po'i srog mthu'i zhal shes gsad thabs rnam pa lngas bstan pa las 'phro can dang 'phrad par shog gi mtha' can /
drag po btsan gyi rkyal 'bud kyi zhal shes yig chung sgrub pa'i zhags grangs spog pa kha bsgyur rnams bstan pa gsang ba'i zhal shes snying ltar chongs las can la 'phrad par shog gi mtha' can| drag po btsan gyi rkyal 'bud kyi yang yig rgya gar gyi ngan sngags gsad pa'i spu gri sdang ba dgra'i gshed ma bla srog rku ba'i man ngag gter nas phyung ba ithi'i mtha' can dang bcas pa legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa la shrI rtags ma gtogs pa yongs rdzogs kyi brgyud pa ni /

'da' phyar /
po dong ba brtson 'grus rdo rje /
jo sras sangs rgyas rin chen /
slob dpon shes rab rgya mtsho /
bla ma bsod nams dbang phyug /
lcang spe pa seng+ge 'bum /
dpal ldan seng+ge /
rin chen bkra shis /
yon tan mgon po /
bla ma gzhon nu dpal /
mus srad ba rdo rje rgyal mtshan /
rgyud gsum smras pa shes rab rin chen /
tshar chen rin po che /
mkhyen brtse /
rta ra pa bsod nams chos 'phel /
sngags 'chang /
dbang phyug rab brtan /
bka' 'gyur ba /
zur chen /
lnga pa chen po /
'jam dbyangs grags pa /
rje mang thos rgya mtsho /
'jam dbyangs bde rdor /
khri ngag dbang mchog ldan /
zhi sprul dge legs rgyal mtshan /
thang sag don grub bstan 'dzin /
chos rdo rje /
klu phug pa rdo rje bde 'byung /
a nu bla ma 'phags pa mchog dga' /
chos rje rin po che blo bzang bstan 'dzin mthu stobs /
rdo rje 'chang bde chen mnyam nyid rdo rje /
khyab bdag brag re bka' 'gyur pa chen po rdo rje 'chang 'phrin las padma kun bzang chos rgyan /
des bdag la'o / /
shrI rtags can rnams kyi lung rgyun sngar ma bzhugs pa phyis su ra brten bla zur rdor 'dzin kun dga' dpal 'byor la zhus pa brgyud pa slar 'tshol dgos zhes chos rje rdo rje 'chang gi gsan yig tu gsungs /
gong gsal bde rtags can rnams lung brgyud lugs gcig ni /
gnas gsar pa bsod nams chos 'phel yan gong ltar la /
de nas ngag dbang chos grags /
ngag dbang rnam rgyal /
kun dga' bkra shis /
mkhan po 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas phun tshogs /
chos rje ye shes 'phrin las /
rje bsod nams chos 'byor /
kun dga' chos 'phel /
mkhan 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas dpal bzang tshul khrims rin chen /
ded dpon dge legs lhun grub /
kun dga' don grub /
dge 'dun rgya mtsho /
bsod nams lhun grub /
bsod nams 'phrin las| rje btsun mkhyen rab bzang po /
rdo rje 'chang bde chen mnyam nyid rdo rje /
khyab bdag brag ri rdo rje 'chang /
des bdag la'o / /
lung gdams skor stag ri dams kyi brgyud lugs gcig ni /
rtogs ldan yon tan mgon po bla chen chos dpal bzang po /
mus srad pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan /
mus chen rnam rgyal dpal bzang /
'khrul zhig dkon mchog bzang po /
tshar chen man 'dra /
gnub lugs gter ma'i lung brgyud ni /
chos sku snang ba mtha' yas /
longs sku padma dbang chen /
sprul sku padma 'byung gnas /
gnub chen sangs rgyas ye shes /
gnub pa tshur ston pa /
gnub ston phug pa 'bar /
de nas rim par sngags 'chang sangs rgyas 'phel /
tshar chen chos kyi rgyal por brgyud pa bzhugs pa bzhin no / /
